  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_6e61c6c1-666b-472b-a5f4-53516846c40f'
      });
    }

      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"

  <span id="freeText6887794765044961213" style="display:none">Starting over sucks.<br /><br />When we moved to West Virginia right before my senior year, I’d pretty much resigned myself to thick accents, dodgy internet access, and a whole lot of boring… until I spotted my hot neighbor, with his looming height and eerie green eyes. Things were looking up.<br /><br />And then he opened his mouth.<br /><br />Daemon is infuriating. Arrogant. Stab-worthy. We do not get along. At all. But when a stranger attacks me and Daemon literally freezes time with a wave of his hand, well, something… unexpected happens. <br /><br />The hot alien living next door marks me.<br /><br />You heard me. Alien. Turns out Daemon and his sister have a galaxy of enemies wanting to steal their abilities, and Daemon’s touch has me lit up like the Vegas Strip. The only way I’m getting out of this alive is by sticking close to Daemon until my alien mojo fades. <br /><br />If I don’t kill him first, that is.</span>

</div>

<span class='likeItContainer' id='like_container_community_question_134905'><a id="like_count_community_question_134905" rel="nofollow" href="/rating/voters/134905?resource_type=CommunityQuestion"><span class="likesCount">21 likes</span></a>&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;<a rel="nofollow" class="jsLike like_it" href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/new?remember=true&amp;return_url=%2Fbook%2Fshow%2F12578077-obsidian">like</a></span>

<div class='allCommunityAnswers'>
<div class='communityAnswer'>
<div class='communityAnswerBody'>
<div class='answererUserIcon'>
<a class="leftAlignedImage userPhoto" href="/user/show/22323214-wray"><img alt="" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/users/1475434372i/22323214._UX100_CR0,16,100,100_.jpg" /></a>
</div>
<div class='communityAnswerTextContainer'>
<span class='communityAnswererName'>
<a href="/user/show/22323214-wray">Wray</a>
</span>
<span class='communityAnswerText'>
<span class="expandableContainer"><span class="truncatedContent">Every paranormal romance/fantasy book is going to have similarities to Twilight. You know why? Because Twilight is in that genre! I have read Twilight<a class="jsShow showAction" href="#">…more</a></span><span class="fullContent">Every paranormal romance/fantasy book is going to have similarities to Twilight. You know why? Because Twilight is in that genre! I have read Twilight and while in the beginning there are similarities; this book is nothing like Twilight. For one it's actually a decent, well thought out story and the main character Katy is actually likable! She's not an annoying damsel in distress like Bella, she actually has a bark to her bite. She quickly became one of my favorite protagonists. The Lux series is wonderful, please do not compare it to the trash in Twilight. Jennifer Armentrout can actually write.<a class="jsHide hideAction" href="#">(less)</a></span></span>
</span>
</div>
</div>

<div id="review_767478671" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/767478671" />
    <a title="Emily May" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4622890-emily-may"><img alt="Emily May" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1528390751p2/4622890.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/767478671?book_show_action=true">Nov 17, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Emily May" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Emily May" href="/user/show/4622890-emily-may">Emily May</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4622890-emily-may?shelf=paranormal-uf">paranormal-uf</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4622890-emily-may?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4622890-emily-may?shelf=2014">2014</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer767478671" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9146168864191137353">Not long ago, someone I know got into a really bad relationship. It was the kind of relationship where the guy was a pretty-faced douchebag who would tell her he loved her one minute and the next he would be making snide remarks about her weight and about her career, or standing her up when they were supposed to be going somewhere. But the worst part of this relationship wasn't him, it was my friend. <br/><br/>Everyone she knew, including me, warned her away from him, told her he was bad and that she dese</span>
  <span id="freeText9146168864191137353" style="display:none">Not long ago, someone I know got into a really bad relationship. It was the kind of relationship where the guy was a pretty-faced douchebag who would tell her he loved her one minute and the next he would be making snide remarks about her weight and about her career, or standing her up when they were supposed to be going somewhere. But the worst part of this relationship wasn't him, it was my friend. <br><br>Everyone she knew, including me, warned her away from him, told her he was bad and that she deserved better... you know, the usual. And she knew exactly who he was, knew that he was playing constant mind games. <b>But she honestly believed that what she put up with was a worthy sacrifice for love</b>. And she honestly believed she could change him. She would say "he's just an immature guy" as we sat with her while she cried because he'd made her feel like shit again. We subtly tried to remind her that there was such a thing as self respect and she was rapidly losing grip on it. <br><br>I sat there and wondered how someone so pretty, smart and full of fiery personality could truly believe this was something normal that she had to accept and get through. But it's when I read books like <i>Obsidian</i> that I receive a painful reminder that this kind of psychology is not only way too frequent, but also constantly reinforced by books selling such relationships as romantic and passionate. Do I need to point out the obvious example?<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1401757859i/9843578.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Some people said this book was another <i>Twilight</i> - complete with sappy heroine, paranormal love interest and a shit ton of angst. Honestly, they insulted <i>Twilight</i> with that one. <b>Give me that creepy creeper called Edward Cullen any day over this rude, arrogant piece of work</b>. I'm pretty sure Edward was actually kinda nice to Bella in his weird archaic "I won't shag you before marriage but I will sneak into your room and watch you sleep because that is totally acceptable and normal" way. <br><br>Daemon, on the other hand, is an arrogant and downright RUDE dickwad. I'm not even going to pretend to understand the attraction because I don't see it. 'kay, he's beautiful, whatever. He also talks to the MC like she's crap he just stepped in, whilst interspersing the abuse with heated kisses and whatnot. There is nothing, <b>NOTHING</b> attractive to me about making out with a guy who insults me and acts like I'm worth less than nothing. I don't get it.<br><br>The heroine - Katy - isn't terrible. She has high points where she pulls out some well-placed snark AND she's a book blogger - woohoo! But she has plenty of eye roll-worthy Mary Sue moments where she frets about her obvious beauty. In the first chapter (I think) she describes herself in a way that is supposed to imply she is somehow plain - with "curvy hips, puffy lips and huge eyes". So... she has big eyes, full lips and curves. Yeah, we really feel your pain, Katy.<br><br>I realise I just basically trashed a book that tops a lot of people's favourite lists - sorry. I am currently working my way through some popular YA that I always meant to read but never did, so that's how I crossed paths with this book after avoiding it for so long. But yeah, guess you figured out this one wasn't for me :)<br><br><a href="http://thebookgeek.co.uk" rel="nofollow noopener">Blog</a> | <a href="https://www.facebook.com/thebookgeekreviews" rel="nofollow noopener">Facebook</a> | <a href="https://twitter.com/thebookgeek01" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a> | <a href="http://instagram.com/emleemay" rel="nofollow noopener">Instagram</a> | <a href="http://mycountryheart.co.uk/" rel="nofollow noopener">Tumblr</a> | <a href="https://www.youtube.com/channel/UCcVsMUSAzMlIKs3nw-xe_nw" rel="nofollow noopener">Youtube</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="9146168864191137353" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <div class="xhr_comment_photo">
    	<a alt="Meg Wolmarans" href="/user/show/112762829-meg-wolmarans"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1586393756p1/112762829.jpg" alt="112762829" /></a>

<span id="freeTextContainer15401942360557737163">I just started this book and I’m like 80 pages in, kinda hooked on the story and yeah bully romances aren’t really my thing anymore now that I’m older</span>
  <span id="freeText15401942360557737163" style="display:none">I just started this book and I’m like 80 pages in, kinda hooked on the story and yeah bully romances aren’t really my thing anymore now that I’m older, more educated and sadly have experiences with real life abuse. But I understand why it’s such a strong seller in these types of novels. I feel like it’s almost taboo now. I have been so pissed off by the victim blaming the MC revives from Daemon. Very yuck. <br /><br />Totally agree with what you’re saying about fantasy romance novels / fiction romance novels perpetuating this unhealthy attraction and acceptance of this behaviour. Admittedly, I did question the first part of your review about your friend being a problem but understood what you meant in the end. Unfortunately, with abusive relationships, I’ve found that no one will leave a situation until they’re good and ready to, despite how far it may go, despite what people tell them. Because that just seems to be a human nature dumb thing. It’s a hard thing to realise but I’ve really had to learn that the hard way. <br /><br />I came to this book series to get over my From Blood and Ash and Kingdom of Flesh and Fire book slump. And I really loved the story, but will always be uncomfortable by the way the love story started. 395 days vibes 😂 <br /><br />I think it’s cool to see that her writing skills improved from this book to her new ones. <br /><br />Anyhow - I needed to see someone else saw what I saw about the toxicity and abuse, so I’m glad others do. I still rate Jen and her story creativity though and will continue with the series if I can. But damn - the victim blaming after her attack really does have me fuming.</span>

<div id="review_1484976377" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1484976377" />
    <a title="Zoë" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9303625-zo"><img alt="Zoë" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1580008879p2/9303625.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1484976377?book_show_action=true">Dec 29, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Zoë" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Zoë" href="/user/show/9303625-zo">Zoë</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1484976377" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16705305133458629505">3.5/5<br/><br/>This book was such a quick, fun read! I haven't read an alien book before, and I found these aliens to be so interesting. Katy was a great main character and I LOVED that she had a book blog. It was a little repetitive at times and the constant bickering between Katy and Daemon, although funny and filled with sexual tension, was almost too much sometimes. However, I'm invested in this story now I will be picking up the next book sometime in the future!</span>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer13115087467002349732"><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/553636.gif' alt='Image Hosted by ImageShack.us' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><br/><i>
  <b>“I have a strange idea that I should test this out.”<br/>“Test what?” My eyes dropped to his lips. I felt myself sway.<br/>“I think you would like to know.” He moved closer, his hand sliding up my arm and resting carefully at the nape of my neck.</b>
</i><br/><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/553637.gif' alt='Image Hosted by ImageShack.us' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><br/><br/><b>Well, now I know why this series is so popular :)<br/>It took me one scene, meeting Daemon, to completely fall in love with him/the book. And it just got better and better! I literally couldn't stop reading and ended up finishing it in the same day I started.<br/>Well t</b></span>
  <span id="freeText13115087467002349732" style="display:none"><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/553636.gif" alt="Image Hosted by ImageShack.us" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><i>
  <b>“I have a strange idea that I should test this out.”<br>“Test what?” My eyes dropped to his lips. I felt myself sway.<br>“I think you would like to know.” He moved closer, his hand sliding up my arm and resting carefully at the nape of my neck.</b>
</i><br><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/553637.gif" alt="Image Hosted by ImageShack.us" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><br><b>Well, now I know why this series is so popular :)<br>It took me one scene, meeting Daemon, to completely fall in love with him/the book. And it just got better and better! I literally couldn't stop reading and ended up finishing it in the same day I started.<br>Well that says a lot :))<br><br><br><br><br>-Here's something you need to know about the STORY-</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/553638.gif" alt="Image Hosted by ImageShack.us" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>Katy and her mom move to Vest Virginia after her father's death, and she meets her gorgeous, irritatingly rude neighbor Daemon.<br><br><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/553639.gif" alt="Image Hosted by ImageShack.us" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>The tension between them is incredible, but with Daemon acting like a jerk, they end up fighting most of the time, and the other times are just swoony as hell!!!!<br><br><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/553640.gif" alt="Image Hosted by ImageShack.us" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>Since Daemon behaves terribly toward Katy, and his sister Dee forces him to be nicer to her, which leads to some very very nice scenes like car-washing, swimming in the lake, the swing scene (*sigh*), the kitchen scene and well basically every scene where Daemon and Katy are together (and there are a LOT of those)<br><br><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/553641.gif" alt="Image Hosted by ImageShack.us" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>One night Daemon saves Katy from a terrible accident and she realises he's not what he seems, he is in fact - an alien!<br><br><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/553642.gif" alt="Image Hosted by ImageShack.us" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>The laptop scene... No comment to that, you just have to read it ;)<br><br><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/553643.gif" alt="Image Hosted by ImageShack.us" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>The ending was awesome, action packed, but also emotional and sweet. And funny. Well it was everything!!! <br><br><br><br><br><br><br><b>-The romance-</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380418054i/827485.jpg" alt="Image Hosted by ImageShack.us" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>*sigh*<br>Well, first thing you need to know is that with Daemon, hearing something romantic come out of his mouth is practically impossible, even though he had his wonderful moments which I treasured because they were rare :D<br>But it was all still there, even though he behaves like a jerk to her, he's still protective, and man, that made some amazingly swoony scenes in here &lt;3<br>And even though I've said it before, every scene with those two was amazing, it was full of tension and butterflies &lt;3<br>Can't wait to see how their relationship moves forward with each book :)<br><br><br><br><br><b>-Daemon-</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380418054ra/827486.gif" alt="Image Hosted by ImageShack.us" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>He's the overprotective brother, trying to prevent Dee (the sister) from forming a friendship with Katy, the new neighbor. <br>He's kind of hot and cold toward her, one moment flirting, the next insulting, probably because he's intrigued by her, but at the same time, he knows what humans can do to him and his family :(<br>As he reveals himself to Katy, he knows he has to keep her safe from his enemies, and they have to spend a lot of time together (ehehehehe).<br><br>Well, for me, Daemon was insta-love. I loved every scene with him, when he was a jerk, when he was swoony and protective, and yeah, even him being so incredibly full of himself :DDD<br>My favorite scene with him was when they were at the lake and she hugged him &lt;3 I don't know why, but he just seemed so vulnerable there, maybe because he's so tough throughout the book, I don't know. <br>Anyway, love love love him!!!<br><br><br><br><br><b>-Katy-</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380418054ra/827487.gif" alt="Image Hosted by ImageShack.us" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>She's a book review blogger, pretty much an ordinary girl, whose life changes completely once her dad dies and she moves to West Virginia with her mom.<br>She becomes friends with her neighbor Dee, but frenemies with Dee's brother Daemon, who tries to push her away from his family, but at the same time flirts like hell with her :D<br>As time goes by, it gets tough for her to fight the attraction, especially because Daemon feels it too, and on top of all that, he has too look after Katy in case his enemies target her.<br><br>For a heroine, she's pretty great :) She gives as good as she gets, and it was so fun to watch the bickering and fighting all the time :) <br>She is brave, and I have to say, I am very very happy with how she deals with the enemies! It surprised me, and I guess that's why I love that fact even more :)<br>The end fight was awesome even though I can't say I understand everything that happened, but I think I'm not supposed to (aka it will probably be explained in the next book).<br><br><br><br><br><b>-Overall feelings about the book-</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380418054ra/827488.gif" alt="Image Hosted by ImageShack.us" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>The pic says it all :DD<br>I devoured this book! I loved every single scene between the MCs, and the good thing is, the book is full of those!!! Honestly, I just can't think of anything that bothered me here or that I didn't like. Anything! <br>Maybe this is just the new fangirl me talking, but I don't know, this book definitely deserves 5 stars from me, and it's going into my bestest of the best shelf :))))<br><br><br><br><b>PS:</b> V... I love you woman! I would've never picked this up if it weren't for you. Yes you told me so, but I just have to say THANK YOU!!! &lt;3<br><br><br><b>PPS:</b> This should be made into a movie.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380418054ra/827489.gif" alt="Image Hosted by ImageShack.us" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><br><br><br></span>

<div id="review_244469332" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/244469332" />
    <a title="Maja (The Nocturnal Library)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4551536-maja-the-nocturnal-library"><img alt="Maja (The Nocturnal Library)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1350750103p2/4551536.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/244469332?book_show_action=true">Dec 08, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Maja (The Nocturnal Library)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Maja (The Nocturnal Library)" href="/user/show/4551536-maja-the-nocturnal-library">Maja (The Nocturnal Library)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4551536-maja-the-nocturnal-library?shelf=are-you-kidding-me">are-you-kidding-me</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4551536-maja-the-nocturnal-library?shelf=what-does-she-see-in-him">what-does-she-see-in-him</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4551536-maja-the-nocturnal-library?shelf=huge-disappointment">huge-disappointment</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4551536-maja-the-nocturnal-library?shelf=i-have-superpowers">i-have-superpowers</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4551536-maja-the-nocturnal-library?shelf=totally-saw-that-coming">totally-saw-that-coming</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4551536-maja-the-nocturnal-library?shelf=postcard-from-outer-space">postcard-from-outer-space</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4551536-maja-the-nocturnal-library?shelf=superbitch">superbitch</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4551536-maja-the-nocturnal-library?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4551536-maja-the-nocturnal-library?shelf=reviewed-in-2011">reviewed-in-2011</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4551536-maja-the-nocturnal-library?shelf=moments-of-great-frustration">moments-of-great-frustration</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer244469332" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2441699818912593584">All my ratings have been pretty high lately, mostly because I choose very carefully what to read next. I value my time too much to purposely read books I know I won’t like. So what on earth possessed me to pick up this book after the <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/9680718.Half_Blood__Covenant___1_' title='Half-Blood (Covenant, #1) by Jennifer L. Armentrout' rel='nofollow noopener'>Half-Blood</a> debacle, I have no idea. <br/><br/>Most of my friends loved Obsidian and I respect that, I really do. I can even see why, the ingredients are all there: a gorgeous, mean guy and a plain, book-nerdish girl, a love-hate relationship between our protagonists, hero’s p</span>
  <span id="freeText2441699818912593584" style="display:none">All my ratings have been pretty high lately, mostly because I choose very carefully what to read next. I value my time too much to purposely read books I know I won’t like. So what on earth possessed me to pick up this book after the <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/9680718.Half_Blood__Covenant___1_" title="Half-Blood (Covenant, #1) by Jennifer L. Armentrout" rel="nofollow noopener">Half-Blood</a> debacle, I have no idea. <br><br>Most of my friends loved Obsidian and I respect that, I really do. I can even see why, the ingredients are all there: a gorgeous, mean guy and a plain, book-nerdish girl, a love-hate relationship between our protagonists, hero’s perky sister that becomes the heroine’s best friend, the evil ex-girlfriend that spits fire every time our heroine gets close, two clueless friends and a mostly absent single parent… need I go on? However, even when you figure all this out, Armentrout finds a way to sneak up on you. Every now and then I’d lose myself in a funny piece of dialogue or an especially steamy scene, but it wouldn’t take long for me to remember what I was really reading and why it was making me so mad. But let’s start at the beginning. <br><br>Three years after the death of her father, Katy’s mother decides that it’s time to move on and that, in order to do that, they need to sell everything they own and move from sunny Florida to a town of about 500 inhabitants in the middle of nowhere, West Virginia. On her first day in the new house, Katy meets her next door neighbors, twins Dee and Daemon. While she and Dee instantly hit it off, Daemon acts like a total jerk and makes some cryptic comments about ‘Katy’s kind’. He is, of course, absolutely gorgeous (<i>Ohmigod, he’s so gorgeous, how could he possibly be attracted to plain ol’ me? I must be imagining things.</i>), and very mysterious. As the time passes, Kat starts noticing that something is not quite right with the way Daemon, Dee and their friends are behaving, and then he saves her from an attacker and well… you know the rest. <br><br>Apparently, aliens are the new vampires. No, seriously. Daemon is Edward 2.0 – a moodier, meaner and prettier version of our dear Mr. Cullen. To be honest, this entire book is just another Twilight rip-off. Not flat-out stolen like Half-Blood, but not that far, either. That alone wouldn’t really upset me much since it's not the first and it certainly won't be the last, but what I found unforgivable was that Armentrout felt the need to make fun of Twilight while writing <b>the exact same story</b>.<br><br><b>And when he spoke, it wasn’t out loud. It was in my head. <i>This is what we look like. We are beings of light. Even in human form, we can bend light to our will.</i> There was a pause. <i>As you can see, I don’t look like a giant insect. Or… sparkle.</i> Even in my head I could hear the disgust on that last one.</b><br><br>See? So rude. It’s true that Daemon doesn’t sparkle, but he IS made of light. Pot, meet kettle. Kettle, you should kick pot’s ass. <br><br>I’m sure this book will have many fans, but I’m afraid my short and turbulent relationship with Ms. Armentrout is now over. <br><br><a href="http://www.thenocturnallibrary.com" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380226536i/681142.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="2441699818912593584" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_1118254870" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1118254870" />
    <a title="Katerina" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5014021-katerina"><img alt="Katerina" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1470667070p2/5014021.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1118254870?book_show_action=true">Nov 29, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Katerina" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Katerina" href="/user/show/5014021-katerina">Katerina</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5014021-katerina?shelf=paranormal">paranormal</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5014021-katerina?shelf=urban-fantasy">urban-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5014021-katerina?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1118254870" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer612169175337324170"><b>Alien.</b> I fell in love with a freaking <b>alien</b>. Not one of those greeny three-eyed creatures but still he <i>is</i> extraterrestrial life. As if book boyfriends from this galaxy weren't enough.<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1441051680ra/16055474.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“Welcome to West Virginia, the land of lost models.”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br/>There was something off with this little Virginia town Katy was forced to move in. Strange things happened, people were supposed to light up like Christmas trees and there was gossip about Men in Black lurking in the streets. And things got even weirder</span>
  <span id="freeText612169175337324170" style="display:none"><b>Alien.</b> I fell in love with a freaking <b>alien</b>. Not one of those greeny three-eyed creatures but still he <i>is</i> extraterrestrial life. As if book boyfriends from this galaxy weren't enough.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1441051680ra/16055474.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“Welcome to West Virginia, the land of lost models.”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br>There was something off with this little Virginia town Katy was forced to move in. Strange things happened, people were supposed to light up like Christmas trees and there was gossip about Men in Black lurking in the streets. And things got even weirder when Katy spent time with her extremely beautiful neighbors, Dee and Daemon. Dee wanted desperately to become friends with Katy, while her brother seemed to consider Katy a stone in his shoe, something unpleasant and annoying. The truth behind this hatred? The Black twins were aliens, hiding from some not so friendly aliens, and Katy found herself involved in a world of secrets, super powers, obsidian knifes and a battle between light and darkness. And a seriously bipolar Daemon.<br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“I was always able to lose myself in reading. Books were a necessary escape I always gladly jumped into headfirst.”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br><b><u>I LOVE <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/12578077.Obsidian__Lux___1_" title="Obsidian (Lux, #1) by Jennifer L. Armentrout" rel="nofollow noopener">Obsidian</a> so, so much</u>.<br>Mystery and paranormal romance combined with sassy characters and humorous dialogues, a healthy dose of tension and agony and sexual frustration and fast paced writing made this book such an enjoyable read!</b> It's my first <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/4476934.Jennifer_L__Armentrout" title="Jennifer L. Armentrout" rel="nofollow noopener">Jennifer L. Armentrout</a> book and I am pleasantly surprised, I can say for sure she gained a new fan! She managed to make aliens fascinating without following the cliches, and her heroes are easily relatable! Kat was an amazing heroine, stubborn and feisty and sarcastic and caring and funny, it's impossible not to love her!<br>And Daemon?<br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“Beautiful face. Beautiful body. Horrible attitude. It was the holy trinity of hot boys.”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br>Totally <b>swoonworthy</b>. An arrogant, hot, overconfident, sex-on-a-stick <b>asshole</b> who gave you heart attacks and took your breath away at once.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380396264ra/763676.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>There were times I wanted to bang his pretty head in a wall and times I wanted him to <s>bang</s> kiss me hard against a wall. He was mostly a rude jerk, but his love towards his sister was touching and the moments he was vulnerable were enough to balance his assholiness.<br>And the scenes between Daemon and Kat?<br><b>Holy Hawt Chemisty, Batman!</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1441052145ra/16055556.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>If you're looking for a good Young Adult novel from a very talented author, then Obsidian is the book for you. After you finish it, you will wish you were kidnapped by aliens (the hot ones who don't look like Chewbacca anyway).</span>
  <a data-text-id="612169175337324170" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_604264607" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/604264607" />
    <a title="Khanh, first of her name, mother of bunnies" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4527753-khanh-first-of-her-name-mother-of-bunnies"><img alt="Khanh, first of her name, mother of bunnies" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1500999223p2/4527753.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/604264607?book_show_action=true">May 01, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Khanh, first of her name, mother of bunnies" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Khanh, first of her name, mother of bunnies" href="/user/show/4527753-khanh-first-of-her-name-mother-of-bunnies">Khanh, first of her name, mother of bunnies</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4527753-khanh-first-of-her-name-mother-of-bunnies?shelf=tstl">tstl</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4527753-khanh-first-of-her-name-mother-of-bunnies?shelf=on-the-run">on-the-run</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4527753-khanh-first-of-her-name-mother-of-bunnies?shelf=twins-triplets-clones">twins-triplets-clones</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4527753-khanh-first-of-her-name-mother-of-bunnies?shelf=why-do-i-hate-myself">why-do-i-hate-myself</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4527753-khanh-first-of-her-name-mother-of-bunnies?shelf=urban-fantasy">urban-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4527753-khanh-first-of-her-name-mother-of-bunnies?shelf=aliens">aliens</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4527753-khanh-first-of-her-name-mother-of-bunnies?shelf=tstl-male">tstl-male</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4527753-khanh-first-of-her-name-mother-of-bunnies?shelf=ya">ya</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4527753-khanh-first-of-her-name-mother-of-bunnies?shelf=siblings">siblings</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer604264607" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3138808292809523655">I want to believe.<br/><br/>I really do. Just following the news these days is enough to make one lose faith in humanity. I really want to believe that there is something out there, god, gods, whatever. Aliens. ANYTHING. I want to feel like there are other creatures out there in this vast universe of ours, with greater knowledge, greater intelligence, and maybe one day they'll grace us with their presence and bestow on us their superior intellect.<br/><br/>I certainly hope those future aliens are more intelligent t</span>
  <span id="freeText3138808292809523655" style="display:none">I want to believe.<br /><br />I really do. Just following the news these days is enough to make one lose faith in humanity. I really want to believe that there is something out there, god, gods, whatever. Aliens. ANYTHING. I want to feel like there are other creatures out there in this vast universe of ours, with greater knowledge, greater intelligence, and maybe one day they'll grace us with their presence and bestow on us their superior intellect.<br /><br />I certainly hope those future aliens are more intelligent than the dumb-as-dirt creatures in <i>Obsidian</i>.<br /><br />Seriously, how stupid can you get? I've never been on the run, I've never had to hide, but if there's some things I've gleaned, it's how NOT to stick out like a sore freaking thumb.<br /><br />First, you find a HUGE goddamn city, like San Francisco, where nobody will even blink if you step out into the street in rainbow-colored pantyhose and an accompanying beard. You do not find a backwoods town where it's likely you're considered outsiders if your grandparents were born the next town over.<br /><br />Secondly, you BLEND IN. 2 pairs of triplets move into town within days of each other? That is not blending in. Supernatural beauty? Not blending in. Names like Daemon? NO. NOT BLENDING IN.<br /><br />Thirdly, you FIT IN. You make friends, you're friendly to people. You do not act like everyone is your enemy and warn off the friendly girl next door just because she wants to know where the closest store is.<br /><br />I just don't understand how this book got so many positive reviews. I get that this is fantasy/sci-fi YA fiction, but there's gotta be a limit to willing suspension of disbelief. For me, there's very little to like about this book. The heroine is all right, but I kind of rolled my eyes at the "I'm a BOOK BLOGGER. I'M SO HIPSTER. I'M A ZOOEY DESCHANEL GEEK GIRL" bit. That's how she seemed to me. She's a fair bit more intelligent than some of the YA fiction heroines I've read, but considering there exists Luce/Bella/etc...that's not saying much. The spaghetti scene was kick-ass, though.<br /><br />I found Daemon to be an enormous asshat for most of the novel. He's hot, sure, but that's it. He's such an unbelievable jerk, and I found Dee to be like the patient wife of an abusive husband, sniveling and simpering and constantly making excuses for her brother's rude, boorish, borderline abusive behavior.<br /><br />And Ms. Armentrout, enough with the 100000x random alien references/foreshadowing in the book already. It's called subtlety.</span>
  <a data-text-id="3138808292809523655" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_218682666" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/218682666" />
    <a title="Steph Sinclair" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4642710-steph-sinclair"><img alt="Steph Sinclair" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1457555690p2/4642710.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/218682666?book_show_action=true">Oct 03, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Steph Sinclair" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Steph Sinclair" href="/user/show/4642710-steph-sinclair">Steph Sinclair</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/14743935-obsidian">review of another edition</a>

          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">I don't know. I just don't know. </span></div>

          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Steph by: </span>
      Tons of avatars on Twitter
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4642710-steph-sinclair?shelf=sci-fi">sci-fi</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4642710-steph-sinclair?shelf=i-need-the-next-book-like-yesterday">i-need-the-next-book-like-yesterday</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4642710-steph-sinclair?shelf=i-blame-twilight">i-blame-twilight</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4642710-steph-sinclair?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4642710-steph-sinclair?shelf=2012-favs">2012-favs</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4642710-steph-sinclair?shelf=all-the-wrong-choices">all-the-wrong-choices</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4642710-steph-sinclair?shelf=smart-heroine">smart-heroine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4642710-steph-sinclair?shelf=best-characters">best-characters</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4642710-steph-sinclair?shelf=ebook">ebook</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4642710-steph-sinclair?shelf=guilty-pleasures">guilty-pleasures</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer218682666" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4487872097073964366"><br/>Actual rating: 3.5 (I think? Geez, I don't know! I just know I liked it a lot, okay?)<br/><br/>Wow. I did not expect to enjoy <em>Obsidian</em> as much as I did. For some reason, I've just been avoiding it, but it was always there in my Twitter and GoodReads feeds. Daemon was frickin' invading my life. Finally, after seeing everyone change their avatars to the Lux series' covers, I felt I had to check it out. Almost all of my friends have given this book anywhere from 3-5 stars, but most averaging around 4. So nat</span>
  <span id="freeText4487872097073964366" style="display:none"><br>Actual rating: 3.5 (I think? Geez, I don't know! I just know I liked it a lot, okay?)<br><br>Wow. I did not expect to enjoy <em>Obsidian</em> as much as I did. For some reason, I've just been avoiding it, but it was always there in my Twitter and GoodReads feeds. Daemon was frickin' invading my life. Finally, after seeing everyone change their avatars to the Lux series' covers, I felt I had to check it out. Almost all of my friends have given this book anywhere from 3-5 stars, but most averaging around 4. So naturally I had to read it to see what the big fuss was about. I was initially wary because I had heard <em>Obsidian</em> was <em>Twilight</em> all over again and we all know how I feel about <em>Twilight</em> and its reincarnations. But surprisingly, I really liked it! Weirdly enough, I <em>could</em> probably go on and on why I didn't like it, but I don't have that urge. I have an urge to hug this book closely because it made me laugh on more than one occasion. Also, Armentrout. I want to hug her too. Because despite <em>Obsidian's</em> headdesk-worthy clichés, I cannot deny... it's an enchanting read. Either that, of I probably shouldn't be drinking while reading.... Ha! Yeah, right.<br><br>Another <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/372071825" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">reviewer said</a>, <em>"It was as if the author felt obligated to fix Twilight catastrophe and tried make it right again"</em> and I completely agree with her. I'll even take it a step further and say it was like Armentrout woke up one day and said, "I'm going to write a book using all the tropes and clichés people usually hate and they're still gonna love the shit out of this book." You might be wondering, "How can one possibly make <em>Twilight</em> better?!" Well, let's take a look at Armentrout's plan for blogosphere domination:<br><br><strong>Step One: Create a likable and relatable main character.</strong><br><br>How do you make a female main character instantly relatable to most of the female blogging community? The answer is so simple I'm honestly kicking myself that I've never thought of it before. You make her one of them. There are so many books I've read where the protagonist is an avid reader. And now I usually find myself going, "YAWN. She can read. Good for her." But not here in <em>Obsidian.</em> Because not only does Katy love to read, but she is a book blogger. Say what? This main character has a... hobby other than staring at her hot next-door neighbor? Nice. Not only that, but Katy is smart, funny, witty and gives Jerkface Daemon a run for his money.<br><br><strong>Step Two: Add a bad boy with two scoops of asshole.</strong><br><br>Ah, the bad boy. Almost every girl goes through the "bad boy phase." It's like a black hole, totally unavoidable, unless you happen to be smarter than the rest of us, in which case, you rock. But there's just something about the thrill of fooling around with someone you know you have no business fooling around with. It can be the best and worst days of your life. That is... until you grow up and get married! XD<br><br><a href="http://cuddlebuggery.com/?attachment_id=12314" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380360549i/711476.png" alt="" width="266" height="246" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Anyway, that's kinda what Daemon is for Katy in <em>Obsidian.</em> He is the irresistible, hot, bad boy who Katy can't deny she's attracted to. But the kicker is that even though Daemon treats her awfully (reasons are revealed in <em>Shadows</em>), she's not one of those heroines that sits back and accepts that. It's one of the first times I've seen a YA heroine differentiate between love and lust. Here's a girl who is saying, "Okay this guy pretty much sets my panties on fire and I would totally exercise him in my bedroom (and possibly in the kitchen by the buttered rolls), but I'm not gonna because he's a complete asshole and I'm better than that." How refreshing!<br><p>And yeah, maybe Daemon is a nice guy underneath all his Jerk-titude, but that doesn't mean Katy has to bend over backwards and ignore his past behavior. Armentrout sets up Daemon's character for redemption because finally someone is saying, "Enough with all the douchebags treating the heroine like shit and still ending up with her in the end just by apologizing." And that is why Obsidian ultimately won me over. At first I couldn't figure out how everyone could love a book when the love interest was a complete tool, but when Katy gave Daemon the one finger salute with a nice "fuck you very much," I knew I was won over.<br><br><strong>Step Three: Choose a paranormal creature that isn't written to death.</strong><br><br>Vampires? Ugh. Werewolves? Old news. Fairies? Boooring! How about something we don't get to see a lot of in YA? Something that will grab your attention! (And I'm not talking about Daemon's... er... friendly nature.)<br><br><a href="http://cuddlebuggery.com/?attachment_id=12342" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380360549i/711477.jpg" alt="" width="300" height="262" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><em>Actually, now that I think of it. That image is pretty accurate. </em><br><br>Maybe I'm not as well read as I thought I was with YA novels, but I don't see a lot of PNR authors tackling aliens. And what a shame! There is so much untapped potential there. In <em>Obsidian</em> you have hundreds of aliens living in West Virginia amongst humans. They're in the schools, holding normal jobs and interacting with humans on a regular basis. So what happens if someone finds out their secret? Awesomeness happens. That's what.<br><br><strong>Step Four: Make overused YA cliché and tropes interesting again.</strong><br><br>Girl moves to a new small town? Check. Heroine doesn't know she's beautiful? Check. Single parent home who has a convenient excuse to leave the heroine alone for long stretches? Check. Paranormal characters hit the genetics jackpot lottery? DOUBLE CHECK. Love interest is so hot he practically melts the heroine's panties off with a grin? Check. Boy save girl from near death experience, therefore revealing his paranormal abilities? Check. Boy tries to deny those abilities? Check. Girl is allergic to his bullshit? Check. I admit, some of these this did bother me, but in the end, it didn't matter too much, especially since there is no insta-love and Katy is frickin' awesome! Hmm... This review turned into one huge lovefest for the MC, Katy. How odd.<br><br><strong>Step Five: Sit back and watch your magic work. Your work here is done.</strong><br><br><a href="http://cuddlebuggery.com/?attachment_id=12343" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380360549i/711478.jpg" alt="" width="374" height="237" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><em> Pinky ring not required, but recommended. </em><br><br>--------------------<br><br>Reaction right after finishing <i>Obsidian:</i><br><br>Gah! This is unexpected. I think my rating is more of a 3.5? 3.75? Got dammit! I don't even know. All I know is my emotions are confused. THEY ARE CONFUSED! This book is like Twilight. But I hate Twilight. Wait... does that mean I <i>like</i> Twilight?! NO. I refuse to believe that. <br><br>Ahhhh! Katy, I love you. Daemon <s>Edward</s>, I want to shake you. <br><br>There are so many things in Obsidian I despise. But I still liked this book. A lot. <br><br>Review to come after I sort out these strange feelings. <br><br><s>And now I'm off to buy Onyx from Amazon even though it's 3am.</s><br><br>Armentrout, what have you done to me? Who am I becoming? Cat woman? (Between you and me, I look pretty damn hot in all leather.) (Okay, that made no sense and was really random.) Gahhhhh!!!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380360549ra/711479.gif" alt="Photobucket Pictures, Images and Photos" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br></p></span>
  <a data-text-id="4487872097073964366" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer752859239" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer5322577738873753404">I can't believe that I haven't reviewed this, because I remember really liking this book. <br/>I thoroughly enjoyed reading Obsidian, and I didn't think I was going to because when I read books about Aliens, I always picture the alien from the film Alien...and that's not a sexy image. <br/><br/>Obsidian starts with our heroine, Katy Swartz moving to West Virginia to start over. <br/>As it turns out, the new house she moves into has a really hot neighbor. <br/>His name his Daemon Black. He's tall and has green eyes. Soun</span>
  <span id="freeText5322577738873753404" style="display:none">I can't believe that I haven't reviewed this, because I remember really liking this book. <br />I thoroughly enjoyed reading Obsidian, and I didn't think I was going to because when I read books about Aliens, I always picture the alien from the film Alien...and that's not a sexy image. <br /><br />Obsidian starts with our heroine, Katy Swartz moving to West Virginia to start over. <br />As it turns out, the new house she moves into has a really hot neighbor. <br />His name his Daemon Black. He's tall and has green eyes. Sounds perfect right? That is until he opened his mouth. <br />Oh and not to forget that he's also an Alien. <br /><br />When I first read this book, I was a little freaked out with myself because I was falling for an Alien...<br />Falling for someone like Christian Grey or Keiran Masters is considered fine, but when you read a book and fall for an Alien, you're kind of like 'wtf is wrong with me?'<br />Now I really liked this book, and I don't read a lot of Science Fiction books. <br />This book is a Paranormal Romance and Mystery. <br />Obsidian has bad-ass characters, tension, it's pretty funny and has also a bit of sexual frustration between our main characters.<br /><br />The Characters<br />Katy was a very likable character. <br />She's stubborn, strong, feisty and hilarious. <br /><br />And Daemon? <br />I want a Daemon for myself<br />I love reading books with guys like Daemon. <br />I don't know what it is with men who are arrogant, infuriating and mean. <br />For me it makes the book more exciting. <br /><br />Jennifer Armentrout...you are a genius!</span>

<div id="review_238220537" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/238220537" />
    <a title="Nicole" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4578380-nicole"><img alt="Nicole" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1442625247p2/4578380.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/238220537?book_show_action=true">Nov 21, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Nicole" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Nicole" href="/user/show/4578380-nicole">Nicole</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

And now I can officially jump on Ms. Armentrout's space ship and enthusiastically follow her anywhere...<br><br> <br><br> <br><br><a href="http://sharearead.com/wp-content/uploads/2012/02/th_hearteyes.gif" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><br><br>I am not usually a big sci-fi reader but there are a few I can like, well I guess now there is one I LOVE and that is the Lux series. Which is actually quite refreshing! Some Authors try to capture true sarcastic personalities and wittiness in their characters but JLA masters it. There is a delicate line that must not crossed for you to truly appreciate the humor in it without turning you off to the character. You just fall for this highly passionate and combustable relationship between Kat and Daemon in <em>Obsidian</em>. You never know if the are going to kiss or kill each other and you can get lost into the journey with them.<br><br>If you have not read this series yet you are seriously missing out! It's extraordinary!<br><br>I also love the quirky personality in Kat and the way she stands up to the enigma that is our sexy arrogant devastatingly handsome Daemon. One of my favorite Kat quotes...<br><br>“Beautiful face. Beautiful body. Horrible attitude. It was the holy trinity of hot boys.”<br><br>And doesn't that just say it all!<br><br>So yes I will be eagerly awaiting the Prequel due out February 21st &amp; the second book Onyx May 15th 2012. As well as purchasing everything that this budding new author has out.<br><br>And the other good news is that I have already stalked her website and google and gotten you all the links you will need to properly follow her along, in what I am sure with be a very long and extremely successful writing career.<br><br>Offical Website of <a href="http://www.jenniferarmentrout.com/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">Jennifer L. <div id="review_398386402" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/398386402" />
    <a title="Kat Kennedy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3270188-kat-kennedy"><img alt="Kat Kennedy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1537750381p2/3270188.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/398386402?book_show_action=true">Aug 23, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kat Kennedy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kat Kennedy" href="/user/show/3270188-kat-kennedy">Kat Kennedy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/13143299-obsidian">review of another edition</a>


          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Kat Kennedy by: </span>
      Stephanie Sinclair
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3270188-kat-kennedy?shelf=the-great-shelf-of-meh">the-great-shelf-of-meh</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3270188-kat-kennedy?shelf=sci-fi-alicious">sci-fi-alicious</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3270188-kat-kennedy?shelf=to-ya-or-not-to-ya">to-ya-or-not-to-ya</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3270188-kat-kennedy?shelf=kat-s-book-reviews">kat-s-book-reviews</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3270188-kat-kennedy?shelf=ya-pnr-maddness">ya-pnr-maddness</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer398386402" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12787644590183069919">Whilst I was aware of this novel before Stephanie read and reviewed it, it didn’t strike me as something that I needed to read until that point. There are many unfavourable comparisons to Twilight floating around. This is not an invalid point.<br/><br/>-6 inhuman teenagers who pretend to be siblings – 1) the love interest (Edward/Daemon) 2) the delicate best friend of the protagonist (Alice/Dee) 3) The bitch sister who doesn’t approve (Rosalie/Ash) 4+5) Background dudes who we don’t see a lot of – one of </span>
  <span id="freeText12787644590183069919" style="display:none">Whilst I was aware of this novel before Stephanie read and reviewed it, it didn’t strike me as something that I needed to read until that point. There are many unfavourable comparisons to Twilight floating around. This is not an invalid point.<br /><br />-6 inhuman teenagers who pretend to be siblings – 1) the love interest (Edward/Daemon) 2) the delicate best friend of the protagonist (Alice/Dee) 3) The bitch sister who doesn’t approve (Rosalie/Ash) 4+5) Background dudes who we don’t see a lot of – one of which is partnered with Alice/Dee.<br /><br />-New girl MC goes to school and meets asshole who is only behaving that way to protect his family.<br /><br />-New girl is with sole parent who provides highly dubious supervision and new girl acts like the parent – cooking, cleaning, shopping etc.<br /><br />-Love interest is devastatingly, unbelievably, inhumanly hot.<br /><br />Blah, blah, blah – we all know the deal. And I knew this going in – but was willing to go with it anyway because, as Steph repeatedly told me, “It’s like she wrote what Twilight SHOULD have been.”<br /><br />To that I say: maybe, yes, kind of, no, a little – but mostly… I guess?<br /><br />So let’s get this out of the way quickly:<br /><br />If you enjoyed Twilight but found the relationship dynamics, i.e. Bella Swan’s permissiveness and stalkish tendencies to be aggravating, then this is your perfect novel. Go forth and multiply, my friend. You will be in heaven.<br /><br />And I can certainly see how this novel could be as addictive as many of my friends say it is. Katy and Daemon scenes, when he’s not being a complete and utter dick, were exceptionally hot. But, to be clear, by scenes I mean “scene” (because there was only one of them – and he went right back to being a dick afterwards) and that wasn’t enough for me.<br /><br />But I could have put that aside, technically, and given this book a higher rating if I hadn’t found myself, for a not insignificant amount of time, bored with the story. Don’t be fooled by the fact that I breezed through it in a few hours. I was trapped in bed all day with sickness. There were a couple of times where the slightest distraction, had one existed, would have fairly swept me off my feet and away from the narrative.<br /><br />Then I started imagining a drinking game for every time I could have come up with a better comeback than Katy. Not an alcoholic one, because I’m sick, but with actual water in the hopes that I wouldn’t dehydrate – which I didn’t. Some of my favourites included: “Glow-stick-for-a-dick”, “Over-grown Fairylight”, “Skinny, limp Twat-bedazzler” and “You have all the charm of a facehugger and only the half the technique, you extraterritorial welfare-mooch!” (this one, clearly, happened after a certain scene that readers will all know and understand my reaction to.)<br /><br />But, and it must be said, having such a strong reaction to the love lives of the characters was a huge indication that I was at least invested, and after reading hundreds and hundreds of books, the ability to still get invested can sometimes be something of a gift. Ultimately I did like Katy even if, as far as I was concerned, she was far too permissive of Daemon’s behaviour. Sticking around and giving him a break when my personal sense of vengeance would have seen a different, more violent and less polite response. And I did, in true guilty-pleasure style, enjoy enough of the book to at least read the free chapters of its sequel, posted at the back.<br /><br />I decided that I will very likely read the next book, because it seemed much more my thing – and I think that interest in reading the subsequent novel is the highest praise I can give.<br /><br />Extra points* to whoever comes up with the best curses to throw at Daemon in the comments!<br /><br /><i>*Points are completely meaningless, have no value, and result in nothing other than my esteem.</i><br /><br />This review can be found on my blog, <a href="http://cuddlebuggery.com/2012/10/book-review-obsidian-by-jennifer-l-armentrout-2/#comments" rel="nofollow noopener">Cuddlebuggery Book Blog</a>.</span>
  <a data-text-id="12787644590183069919" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_446910468" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/446910468" />
    <a title="Debra" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13247178-debra"><img alt="Debra" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1473718933p2/13247178.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/446910468?book_show_action=true">Nov 02, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Debra" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Debra" href="/user/show/13247178-debra">Debra</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/14743935-obsidian">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=alpha-male">alpha-male</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=horror-supernatural">horror-supernatural</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=young-adult-fiction">young-adult-fiction</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=swoonworthy-male-lead">swoonworthy-male-lead</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer446910468" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer326035376827280117"><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"If she was mine, I'd cherish every inch of her. And I wanted to. Now."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380396264i/763672._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>HOLY ALIEN HOTNESS.</b><br/><br/>After hearing nothing but positive things about this series, I thought it was about time I'd give it a try myself to find out what all the hype was about and WOW... I'm SO GLAD I finally started it!!! There was never a dull moment in this first part of the series and once I got into the story, I ended up devouring it! I'm pretty sure this will quickly become my new favorite YA series once I cont</span>
  <span id="freeText326035376827280117" style="display:none"><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"If she was mine, I'd cherish every inch of her. And I wanted to. Now."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380396264i/763672._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>HOLY ALIEN HOTNESS.</b><br><br>After hearing nothing but positive things about this series, I thought it was about time I'd give it a try myself to find out what all the hype was about and WOW... I'm SO GLAD I finally started it!!! There was never a dull moment in this first part of the series and once I got into the story, I ended up devouring it! I'm pretty sure this will quickly become my new favorite YA series once I continue with the rest of it!!! Although it's considered to be YA, I felt it had a much more mature feeling to it. I loved the characters, the original storyline and the engaging writing style and well, <b>Daemon Black is one hot alien you just HAVE to meet...</b><br><br><br><b>
  <u>THE STORY</u>
</b><br><br><i>Starting over is never easy...</i><br><br>After Katy's father passed away, her mother decides it's best for them to leave the house they used to live in and move some place new. They leave Florida and decide to start over in a small town in West Virginia. Moving into a new town and enrolling in a new school for her senior year, isn't easy... But what's worse is having a new neighbor who isn't very welcoming to her at all.<br><br><b>
  <i>"I thought people in small towns were supposed to be nice, not act like the son of Satan."</i>
</b><br><br>While struggling to find her place in this strangely populated town, Katy also has to find a way to cope her handsome but extremely arrogant neighbor <i>Daemon Black</i>. Although Katy quickly becomes friends with Daemon's sister Dee, Daemon keeps treating her like she doesn't belong is this town, which makes her feel like something is off about him... And then she discovers the neighbors next door are nothing she could have ever expected; they're aliens.<br><br><br><b>
  <u>KATY SWARTZ</u>
</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380396264i/763673.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>"The day my internet was hooked up was better than having a hot guy check our my butt and ask for my phone number."</i>
</b><br><br>I really loved Katy's personality. She's down to earth, funny, sarcastic and full of witty remarks. Plus, she's also a book nerd which made her all the more easy to relate with. I loved that the story was written in her point of view, because being inside her head was <i>never</i> boring. She's a strong character and I admired that she stood up for herself so well. Especially against someone like Daemon...<br><br><br><b>
  <u>DAEMON BLACK</u>
</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380396264i/763674._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>"Beautiful face. Beautiful body. Horrible attitude. It was the holy trinity of hot boys."</i>
</b><br><br><p><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380396264ra/763675.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Yes, Daemon is HOT as hell BUT at the same time he's also infuriatingly annoying. At first I didn't know whether to love him or hate him...<br></p><p><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380396264ra/763676.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And neither did Katy! Daemon constantly switches his attitude from hot to cold and back again. Most of the time, he treats her like his number one enemy and he even tries to keep her away from his sister, in fear of them becoming to close. <br><br><b><i>"To Daemon, my arrival was the beginning of the end. The apocalypse. Kat-mageddon."</i></b><br><br>Most of the time Katy and Daemon don't get along AT ALL. But since, Katy has become best friends with Daemon's twin sister Dee (who's character I absolutely loved btw!), they are forced to spent some time together. Whenever they do meet though, Daemon manages to infuriate the hell out of Katy.<br><br><i><b>"I'd always avoided confrontation in the past, but this guy was flipping my bitch switch like nothing else."</b></i><br><br>I loved the playful banter between the two of them. It kept the story interesting and refreshing and it provided some hilarious and highly entertaining moments...<br><br><b><i>"You're such an ass. Has anyone ever told you that?"<br>He flashed a genuinly amused smile. "Oh, Kitten, every single day of my blessed life."</i></b><br><br>And even though they're constantly arguing, they also share a few intimate moments where Daemon shows the "real" him and he becomes a much nicer version of himself.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380396264i/763677.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Daemon tries to keep his distance from Katy, but because he's had to save her life a few times, she carries a glow of energy around her that the Arum, the Luxen's greatest enemy, can detect. Therefore, Daemon is "forced" to spend time with Katy and protect her from potential attacks until the effect from his alien mojo has faded away. Whenever they're around each other, there's a tension in the air and it's obvious they're attracted to each other...<br><br><b><i>"Holy Hawt Chemistry, Batman!"</i></b><br><br>And when they *finally* kiss, the chemistry is off the charts!!!</p><p><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380396264ra/763678.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The entire story is written in Katy's POV but at the end of the book we also get a few chapters from Daemon's POV and for that I am VERY grateful. They really show that despite his cockiness, he actually had a good reason for acting the way he did.<br><br>So, Daemon, despite some of your more "jerkish" moves... </p><p><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380396264ra/763679.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><br><b>Luckily, this first part of the series does not end with a cliffhanger, but the ending still makes me want to read the next part of the series very soon!!!</b><br><br>HIGHLY RECOMMENDED to anyone who enjoys YA paranormal stories!!!<br><br><br>~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~<br></p><p>
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380396264ra/763680.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  <br>
  <br>
</p><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"I won't hurt you, Kat." His tone was softer, but still laced with fury as he tried to control me without doing any real damage. "I could never hurt you."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><br><b>4.5 STARS.</b><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="326035376827280117" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/228098016" />
    <a title="Maria " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5769334-maria"><img alt="Maria " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1600318539p2/5769334.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/228098016?book_show_action=true">Oct 27, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Maria " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Maria " href="/user/show/5769334-maria">Maria </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer228098016" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14164532568252427570"><br/><blockquote>
  <i> “So the dickhead had a name. Daemon—seemed fitting.” </i>
</blockquote><br/><br/>What do you get when you combine a shy girl from Florida and a sexy, arrogant next door neighbor? <br/><br/>You get <b> OBSIDIAN!</b><br/><br/><b>What do I think about this book?</b><br/><br/><a href='http://media.photobucket.com/image/fangirl%20gif/princessaili/gif%20macros/fangirl.gif?o=1' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>

</a><br/><br/><a href='http://media.photobucket.com/image/fangirl%20gif/rosaxx50/fangirl.gif?o=10' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <span>[image error]</span>
</a><br/><br/><a href='http://photobucket.com/images/fangirl%20gif' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
