</a><br/><br/>Okay! I think that shows just about how much I love this book! And how absolutely crazy I am of it but at first I didn’t really feel that way towards it.<br/><br/><b>INITIAL THOUGHTS</b><br/><br/>A lot of my goodreads friends recommended this book to me but I was like “Oh no! Aliens?”. Then I sa</span>
  <span id="freeText14164532568252427570" style="display:none"><br><blockquote>
  <i> “So the dickhead had a name. Daemon—seemed fitting.” </i>
</blockquote><br><br>What do you get when you combine a shy girl from Florida and a sexy, arrogant next door neighbor? <br><br>You get <b> OBSIDIAN!</b><br><br><b>What do I think about this book?</b><br><br><a href="http://media.photobucket.com/image/fangirl%20gif/princessaili/gif%20macros/fangirl.gif?o=1" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/488303.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><a href="http://media.photobucket.com/image/fangirl%20gif/rosaxx50/fangirl.gif?o=10" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <span>[image error]</span>
</a><br><br><a href="http://photobucket.com/images/fangirl%20gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/282765.gif" alt="fangirl gif Pictures, Images and Photos" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Okay! I think that shows just about how much I love this book! And how absolutely crazy I am of it but at first I didn’t really feel that way towards it.<br><br><b>INITIAL THOUGHTS</b><br><br>A lot of my goodreads friends recommended this book to me but I was like “Oh no! Aliens?”. Then I saw a lot of good reviews about it so I decided to grab a copy but still haven’t read it I wasn’t interested. But then this June I just had the urge to open it up and read it. <br>After just reading a few pages I was in love!<br>It was like love at first sight!<br><br><b>THE GIRL</b><br><br>Katy!<br>I love you girl! Well of course not as much as I love beeeepp <s>Daemon</s> but yeah she’s a good and very amusing character.<br>Why?<br>First, she loves books and she blogs. You don’t often get kickass characters who read and blog right?<br>Also she was not like most of the other female lead characters in YA books nowadays who are so dependent on their guys that it almost makes me gag just by reading about it.<br>I hate needy, reliant female characters and Katy was <b>NOT</b> one of them.<br>And I seriously enjoyed reading about her because she doesn’t take crap from ahhheeem <s>Daemon</s> who was also well a jerk most of the time.<br>Plus this girl was not stupid. <br>Yeah well she doesn’t have super powers (and most of the time I think she honestly forget this. Hahaha ) but she thinks before she acts and she thinks about the welfare of other too like.<br>She doesn’t ogle. Even though Daemon was hot as hell she didn’t. She had thoughts yes but she doesn’t show it to Daemon well expect for the… Hahaha. I wouldn’t want to say when because that would obviously ruin the surprise!<br><br><b>THE GUY</b><br><br>OHHH I could feel myself fangirling again!!!!<br><br><a href="http://media.photobucket.com/image/fangirl%20gif/Mojjochan/EMO-OPI-GIF/tumblr_lmlehkVnSO1qavzki.gif?o=26" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/267818.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Oh Daemon! Where were you when I fell in love with Ash!<br>You bad boy! You’re making me so unfaithful!<br>Seriously, once you get a piece of Daemon you’ll definitely ask for more.<br>Daemon’s character for me was so out of this world. Well technically he is really from out of this world.<br>He was obnoxious, rude, arrogant and mean. But one thing is for sure though, <b>DAEMON BLACK IS THE HOTTEST GUY I’VE EVER READ!</b><br>It infuriate me sometimes that he could be such an asshole when he’s around Katy but when you read his short POV’s at the end of the book you’ll find out why he has to be that way.<br>All I could really say is he’s more than that.<br>He is more than the arrogant jerk that he puts off in front of everybody.<br><br><b>DAEMON + KATY = UNDENIABLE CHEMISTRY</b><br><br>They are mean to each other most of the time and I find it really enjoyable to read.<br>I like how Katy stands up for herself even when Daemon embarrass her she still stick to her guns and stand up tall.<br>There was really something there whether they deny it or not.<br>Whether Daemon tries to fight it off by being a douche, he won’t be able to keep that for long.<br>They’re just so cute.<br><br><b> MORE THOUGHTS </b><br><br>The plot for me was well executed. <br>I mean it wasn’t fast paced as I would have wanted it to but everything seem to fall into place. <br>There were no dull moments nor where there moments that you wouldn’t understand what was going on.<br>Ms. Armentrout made sure that the readers would devour every scene and every word and every action of the characters.<br>And she was successful in doing that.<br>I read her other book but I wasn’t as into it as much as this book.<br>This book was awesome! I couldn’t even find the right words.<br><br><a href="http://media.photobucket.com/image/fangirl%20gif/rosaxx50/fangirl.gif?o=10" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <span>[image error]</span>
</a><br><br>This book gives new light to Aliens. <br>Well I did like <b> I am Number Four </b> but I don’t think it was as enjoyable to read as this one.<br>And the writing was just so fluid for me.<br>It was as if a teenage girl was really telling the story. It was just so authentic. <br><br><b> TO RECOMMEND OR NOT TO RECOMMEND</b><br><br>TO RECOMMEND DEFINITELY! <br>I would have to say I enjoyed everything about this book start from the characters, the setting, the pace, the plot, the writing, the humor, everything. <br>I couldn’t find a miss from my part.<br>It was all too perfect for me.<br>I mean you all might not agree with me but yeah I think this book was just perfect.<br>And also did I mention that I love Daemon?! :D<br><br><a href="http://photobucket.com/images/ovaries" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380361995ra/713085.gif" alt="omg fangirl ovaries Pictures, Images and Photos" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b> A PERFECT 5! Or 10! Or 100! :D</b></span>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

<span id="freeTextContainer2379978732162639106"><i>“Beautiful face. Beautiful body. Horrible attitude. It was the holy trinity of hot boys.”</i><br/><br/>Jennifer L. Armentrout writes the best make-out scenes ever. No shit.<br/>Nevertheless the rest of the book was enjoyable, too. Most of the time I spent reading <i>Obsidian</i>, was with a big fat grin plastered on my face.<br/>What bothered me was how obvious and predictable the situation was: Katy being the new girl in town, Daemon Black being at least as obviously dark and sexy and mysterious as his name, the two of them </span>
  <span id="freeText2379978732162639106" style="display:none"><i>“Beautiful face. Beautiful body. Horrible attitude. It was the holy trinity of hot boys.”</i><br /><br />Jennifer L. Armentrout writes the best make-out scenes ever. No shit.<br />Nevertheless the rest of the book was enjoyable, too. Most of the time I spent reading <i>Obsidian</i>, was with a big fat grin plastered on my face.<br />What bothered me was how obvious and predictable the situation was: Katy being the new girl in town, Daemon Black being at least as obviously dark and sexy and mysterious as his name, the two of them "hating" and falling for each other, and the big secret that Daemon and his family tried to hide from Katy.<br />There were so many <i>Twilight</i> similarities, but that didn't stop me from reading, since it was light and funny and really entertaining.<br />I admit, I also kinda fell for Daemon, despite his stupid name and attitude.<br />And now I can't wait to get my fingers on the sequels.<br /><br /><a href="https://www.instagram.com/fantasticbooksandwheretofindem/" rel="nofollow noopener">Find more of my books on Instagram</a></span>

<div id="review_1484900637" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1484900637" />
    <a title="Emer (A Little Haze)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4629647-emer-a-little-haze"><img alt="Emer (A Little Haze)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1589390599p2/4629647.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1484900637?book_show_action=true">Dec 29, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Emer (A Little Haze)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Emer (A Little Haze)" href="/user/show/4629647-emer-a-little-haze">Emer (A Little Haze)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4629647-emer-a-little-haze?shelf=read2016">read2016</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4629647-emer-a-little-haze?shelf=trashtastic">trashtastic</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4629647-emer-a-little-haze?shelf=reviewed">reviewed</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4629647-emer-a-little-haze?shelf=abn-readalongs">abn-readalongs</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4629647-emer-a-little-haze?shelf=read2017">read2017</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4629647-emer-a-little-haze?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4629647-emer-a-little-haze?shelf=books-owned-all-formats">books-owned-all-formats</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4629647-emer-a-little-haze?shelf=4stars">4stars</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1484900637" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7200109011646791706"><b>second reading: October 2017</b><br/><br/><br/>Yup. This is still insanely addictive. <br/>Daemon is still insanely hot.<br/>It is still insanely ridiculous. <br/>Also insanely written!<br/>But most importantly I am still insanely in love with this book. <br/>#SorryNotSorry<br/><br/><br/>It is utterly trashtastic but it's hilarious. Like I legit burst out laughing at so much stuff when reading this. It's filled with innuendo and low key digs at Twilight. I mean it's basically a homage at times. <br/>But where it truly kicks Twilight's butt is the MC Katy... </span>
  <span id="freeText7200109011646791706" style="display:none"><b>second reading: October 2017</b><br><br><br>Yup. This is still insanely addictive. <br>Daemon is still insanely hot.<br>It is still insanely ridiculous. <br>Also insanely written!<br>But most importantly I am still insanely in love with this book. <br>#SorryNotSorry<br><br><br>It is utterly trashtastic but it's hilarious. Like I legit burst out laughing at so much stuff when reading this. It's filled with innuendo and low key digs at Twilight. I mean it's basically a homage at times. <br>But where it truly kicks Twilight's butt is the MC Katy... <br><br><br>Katy is a fabulous main character. She is sassy, spunky, feisty, vulnerable, fierce... I mean don't get me wrong we are still talking about a trashtastic book so she's not entirely without a dusting of snowflakes of the spechul variety. But she's not a character that will make you want to shoot yourself to spare you from her repeated idiocy unlike a bazillion other YA spechul snowflakes. So thumbs up for Katy. <br><br><br>Daemon is the king of emotional fuckwits but he's such a pretty king that you won't care. I mean you might think you have standards and are above all this abs stuff 🙄🙄 but, case in point, you should just see what this book has done to my GR friend Aimee, a sworn enemy of these trashtastic books who is now SO addicted she's already on the third book of this series!!!!<br>Am I smug for recommending this to my book group and for having pretty much all of them fall desperately in love with my Daemon.... <br><b>YOU BETCHA I AM SMUG AF </b>😂😂😂<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1509064578i/24288696.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Btw ladies of ABN. I saw Daemon first so he's ALL mine <br><br><br>Anyway this is fast paced and filled with bonkers action to keep you wanting to turn those pages. Okay it's got TERRIBLE scientific explanations that will make you cry with laughter when anything regarding the *science* behind the alien "stuff" is mentioned but honestly I didn't read this book for a science lesson. I mean I can recommend some great science books to you if you want but certainly not this 😂😂😂<br><br><br>But the best part of this book is the relationship between Katy and Daemon. The chemistry between them is off the charts smokin' hot! I mean obvs they hate each other IMMEDIATELY but we all know not really and truly... Confession! The 'hate-each-other-at-first-sight-even-though-you're-insanely-attracted-to-the-other-person' is probably my absolute FAV romance trope. I just love it and can never get enough of it BUT only if it's done well. And it is done sooooooo well here. Like you will practically scream at this book waiting for them to either punch each other or make out. It's FAB-U-LOUS 💁🏼<br><br><br>So after a second reading has my four star rating changed to something lower??<br><br>HELL TO THE NO!!!!!<br><br>YOU KEEP ALL THOSE FOUR STARS DAEMON BABY!!!! And you can have an extra half one for the LOLs <br><br><b>four and a half <i>I-have-never-been-so-easily-or-highly-entertained</i> stars</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1509064578i/24288697._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><br><br>*****<br><br><br><br><br><b>DAEMON MY BABY I HAVE COME BACK TO YOU!!!!!</b><br><br>Currently reading this little beauty for the second time with my book group. So proud that I'm the one who suggested this trash-fest of deliciousness. BRING ON THE ABS 😂😂😂😂<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1509064578i/24288698._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><br>*****<br><br><br><br><br><b>FIRST READING: February 2016</b><br><br><br><b>Gaaaaah!!!</b> So Obsidian... wow this book, THIS BOOK!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!! So it was basically like the book version of crack!!!!!!!!!!! Or at least a caffeine fix (let’s try not to be too dramatic for once Emer…) Anyway ADDICTIVE!!!! YES!!!!... I am tooooooootally hooked on this book and these characters.... Aaaaaaaaaaaaaaand… <b>I WANT MORE!!!!</b> <br><br><br>It's all this super-addictive teen drama of hot aliens, dangerous moody, <i>*cough*</i> swoony <i>*cough cough*</i> boys and lust and excitement and... like I said before… <br><u>I WANT MORE!!!</u> <br><i>GIMME GIMME GIMME!!!!! <br><b>WANT WANT WANT!!!!</b></i> <br><br><br>Good gosh do I <u>HATE</u> myself for saying this because... well it means I am a walking, talking cliché but Daemon... I love you.... *swooning heart eyes* <b>DAMN IT!!!</b> I fell for the moody, mysterious boy who treats the lead girl, Katy, like crap...... I mean he's basically an <u>
  <i>utter</i>
</u> <b>tosser!!!</b>... <i>WHAT IS WRONG WITH ME?????</i> Grrrrrrrr!!!! I just need to read ALL the books in this series like right this minute. If I could do some weird alien juju and absorb them into my own brain just immediately or something..... <b>AHHHHHHH THIS WAS JUST TOO GOOD!!!!</b><br><br><br>Ok breathe, calm down...think logically. Well it's a four star book for the thrills and spills and for turning my girlish head like that! There aren't any amazingly quotable passages, the writing doesn't exactly knock my socks off, there are clichés aplenty, predictable storylines and plot development.... but Daemon makes up for <i>
  <b>all</b>
</i> of that!!! Oh I'd like to have been Katy and move next door to a hot bunch of aliens like that. This TOTALLY reminded me of Roswell High... you remember that series???? Max and Liz making googly eyes at each other and being all connected... *teenage sigh* I love that show... <b>I love this even more!!!!</b> <br><br><br>So guess what……….. I loved this!!!!!!!!! <b>*nods enthusiastically*</b> It was a fun, flirty and very easy read. I read it in hospital while waiting to be called down to theatre for surgery so any book that can completely distract someone from an event like that deserves some praising!!!<br><br><b>Four VERY HAPPY stars</b><br><br>Roll on the rest of the Lux series!!!</span>
  <a data-text-id="7200109011646791706" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

    <a title="❥ KAT ❥ Kitty Kats Crazy About Books" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6245313-kat-kitty-kats-crazy-about-books"><img alt="❥ KAT ❥ Kitty Kats Crazy About Books" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1582051737p2/6245313.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3128223100?book_show_action=true">Jan 06, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="❥ KAT ❥ Kitty Kats Crazy About Books" class="user" itemprop="url" name="❥ KAT ❥ Kitty Kats Crazy About Books" href="/user/show/6245313-kat-kitty-kats-crazy-about-books">❥ KAT ❥ Kitty Kats Crazy About Books</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6245313-kat-kitty-kats-crazy-about-books?shelf=paranormal">paranormal</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3128223100" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8846857654682150632"><a href='https://ibb.co/MSkg3sG' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1578458142i/28735021._SX540_.jpg' alt='OBSIDIAN' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><b>'OBSIDIAN'</b> is the first full length PRN | FANTASY book in new to me author Jennifer L. Armentrout's 'LUX' series. <br/><br/><b>Hello January</b><br/><br/>Twice a month I'm going to fulfill my own reading challenge and that is to read something new/something old/something out of my comfort zone/a new genre/something I wouldn't usually even give a second glance too. A non ARC!!<br/><br/>So this book is January's challenge!! It's a newish genre to me, it's an oldie/a new author to me/and has been recommended to me numerous times!!</span>
  <span id="freeText8846857654682150632" style="display:none"><a href="https://ibb.co/MSkg3sG" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1578458142i/28735021._SX540_.jpg" alt="OBSIDIAN" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><b>'OBSIDIAN'</b> is the first full length PRN | FANTASY book in new to me author Jennifer L. Armentrout's 'LUX' series. <br><br><b>Hello January</b><br><br>Twice a month I'm going to fulfill my own reading challenge and that is to read something new/something old/something out of my comfort zone/a new genre/something I wouldn't usually even give a second glance too. A non ARC!!<br><br>So this book is January's challenge!! It's a newish genre to me, it's an oldie/a new author to me/and has been recommended to me numerous times!! <br><br><a href="https://imgbb.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1578458727i/28735045.jpg" alt="2ir3yw5" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>HOLY CRAP</b> There has to be something in the water 💦<br>because <b>I SHIT YOU NOT</b> I loved this! Who would’ve thought! It’s not a genre I’d gravitate to (like ever), it’s one I’d not even glance at, I'm not gonna lie when peeps were all like <i>"OMG you are going to LOVE this one."</i> I seriously kind of snorted like a pig!! And thought 'whatever' I’m a romance kind of gal! But this surprised me, I can’t even explain why I loved it so much! It’s beyond unique, and utterly unputdownable, I devoured this! <br><br>It has those 'Twilight' feels to it, though this hotty on the cover is an alien, yep an alien!! 👽He's not the ET phone home type of Alien either. Thank god for small mercies because just no that would've been too creepy!! <br><br>Now onto our heroine, oh my god did I love her, she had me giggling non stop!! She's who we all could relate to, a book blogger, a book nerd, a tough sassy mouthed kind of girl who stood her ground in every situation she found herself in!! She even gave Daemon a run for his money!<br><br>I can honestly say that I’m not in love with Daemon’s character, because I guess Aliens are more like humans than I thought! He was hot and cold, went backwards and forwards more times than I can count, he was a bit of an alpha A-Hole really, but he does have me coming back for more! If I have no arc commitments I’m jumping on the next book!<br><br><blockquote>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer246184907" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10380154741469478366">First, a caveat: I did not enjoy this book. The following is my honest opinion, however I mean no disrespect to those of my friends who liked it. <br/><br/>Just to be clear, I approached Obsidian optimistically, looking for something fun and entertaining to read. Because <i>hot alien</i> spells fun, am I right? Particularly on the heels of a couple of quite emotionally taxing books. <br/><br/>Well, apparently I should have checked myself before I wrecked myself, and paid heed to those little warning bells in the synopsis:</span>
  <span id="freeText10380154741469478366" style="display:none">First, a caveat: I did not enjoy this book. The following is my honest opinion, however I mean no disrespect to those of my friends who liked it. <br /><br />Just to be clear, I approached Obsidian optimistically, looking for something fun and entertaining to read. Because <i>hot alien</i> spells fun, am I right? Particularly on the heels of a couple of quite emotionally taxing books. <br /><br />Well, apparently I should have checked myself before I wrecked myself, and paid heed to those little warning bells in the synopsis: “Arrogant.” “Stab-worthy.” Attaching these descriptors to the love interest should have tipped me off that at least part of this story really wasn’t going to gel with me. <br /><br />Overall though, I am more disappointed than anything, because I feel that there was a lot going for this premise. It makes me sad to see such potential and a fun idea be eclipsed by a banal romance that draws so heavily on YA paranormal tropes and clichés. <br /><br />There was promise in Katy. Despite her familiar casting as the new girl in town who has no idea that she’s pretty – Katy has personality, interests, a good relationship with her mother and is generally down to earth. She wasn’t a vapid, self-insert type of character, which was a positive sign. Sure, the “bookish” type heroine feels a little tired these days, but Katy seemed like a strong enough character to carry this story. <br /><br />Enter the <s>hot alien</s> mysterious boy next door. <br /><br />From this point on, while there were flashes of the book I thought this would be, it started to take a disappointingly familiar path. I felt my enjoyment steadily decline, to the point where I was frankly just angry and frustrated. <br /><br />Having the protagonist state upfront that the love interest is a “douche” does not give said love interest carte blanche to go around committing Random Acts of Assholery in the name of Broody Hotness. The fact that the protagonist acknowledges the bad behaviour does not suddenly make it acceptable. Beating readers to the punch of calling out the love interest as a jerk does not award him a “Be A Jerk For Free” card.<br /><br />Honestly, it makes me just plain cranky even after Katy recognises that Daemon is a douche, we are supposed to simply swallow this and understand her poor choices because he’s so allegedly “intriguing” and has a smokin’ bod. Demeaning, obnoxious behaviour is still demeaning and obnoxious any way you slice it. No matter how rock hard his abs, how finely chiselled his jaw, how piercing his eyes, I don’t find it hot. Acknowledgment and justification are <i>not</i> the same thing.<br /><br />In short, and to channel Cher Horowitz of Clueless: “So okay, I don't want to be a traitor to my generation and all but I don't get YA love interests today. I mean, come on, they just turn up to the door shirtless and throw around some insults and make suggestive comments - ew - and then ignore you completely and like, we're expected to swoon? <i>I don't think so</i>.”<br /><br />Unfortunately, I suspect that there is an Edward Cullen style “I’m horrible to you because I secretly love you and I can’t admit it” dynamic at play here. I can’t help but speculate that beneath Daemon’s outward displays of arrogance and kick-to-the-crotch-worthy insults, Armentrout is going to slowly reveal a tender heart that beats with genuine love for Katy. <br /><br />Please. <br /><br />While there are some scenes that are quite funny and/or tense, and the make-out moments are well-written, I have to say that I feel the whole thing is let down by a rather formulaic plot. A few sharply rendered, interesting characters are counter balanced with some that feel like caricatures. The pacing, particularly of the climax, is gripping and fast – yet the events themselves feel all too familiar. <br /><br />Given the fact that a book I wanted to find entertaining yet left me feeling wound up and annoyed, I think it’s safe to say that it wasn’t for me. <br /><br />So if anyone can rec me a good alien book, please do. I’m all ears<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="10380154741469478366" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_228406641" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/228406641" />
    <a title="Taneika" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5591031-taneika"><img alt="Taneika" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1564410672p2/5591031.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/228406641?book_show_action=true">Oct 28, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Taneika" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Taneika" href="/user/show/5591031-taneika">Taneika</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback " href="/book/show/25277070-obsidian">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer228406641" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7929817682005585776">Well, looks like I'm a black sheep for this one guys. <br/><br/>I did not go into this book expecting wonderful prose or a particularly moving story. I went into this book expecting pure fun, guilty-pleasure like entertainment and a hot alien.<br/>All I got was a hot alien.<br/>(Maybe I could put that on a t-shirt, "I read this book and all I got was this hot alien tshirt" and then just slap a picture of Daemon Black's face/abs on the back)<br/><br/>Obsidian was a novel I avoided for a very long time as it sounded like somet</span>
  <span id="freeText7929817682005585776" style="display:none">Well, looks like I'm a black sheep for this one guys. <br /><br />I did not go into this book expecting wonderful prose or a particularly moving story. I went into this book expecting pure fun, guilty-pleasure like entertainment and a hot alien.<br />All I got was a hot alien.<br />(Maybe I could put that on a t-shirt, "I read this book and all I got was this hot alien tshirt" and then just slap a picture of Daemon Black's face/abs on the back)<br /><br />Obsidian was a novel I avoided for a very long time as it sounded like something I would despise. I finally bit the bullet and read it and while I didn't hate it, I certainly didn't enjoy it. <br /><br />I'm not going to sit here and draw all the parallels to Twilight because I'm pretty sure every man and their dog has come to that conclusion. The parallels to Twilight isn't even my main problem with this book, in fact I found it to be better written and marginally more entertaining than Twilight. My main problem with this book is that it was <b>boring</b>. I found myself putting this down and not really having the desire to pick it back up because I just didn't care. The plot was so damn predictable and I didn't feel any sense of urgency or excitement in it at all. I went into this thinking this would at least be entertaining and fun to read even if it wasn't a work of art, but I didn't even feel a little entertained by the story for the most part. Sure, there are parts where it's exciting and there's a few hot scenes between Daemon and Katy because they do have some pretty great chemistry, but those weren't enough for me to love this book.<br /><br />I actually really liked Katy, despite finding her a bit annoying at times. Not only is she a book blogger in which I found myself reminiscing about how book blogging used to be a few years ago, and I found her much more relatable in that she would come home after a bad day, see a parcel of books waiting for her and she would get super excited. But she was also snarky, aggressive and different to a lot of other YA heroines. As for Daemon, the alien who is super hot and infuriating etc, I found him hotter toward the end of the story, but for the most part I just didn't give a shit about him at all. The other characters were all cardboard cutouts and essentially added nothing to the story.<br /><br />The writing was okay and I did find this super easy to read in the parts I wasn't bored out of my mind.<br />Even the antagonists were hilariously bad. Like, there's this one scene where THEY'RE ACTUALLY MAKING HISSING SOUNDS WHEN THEY SPEAK AND I COULDN'T CONTAIN MY LAUGHTER. It was so absurd, it was hilarious. The antagonists are supposed to be this huge threat and everything but oh my god, they had no substance whatsoever which just ended up making them seem more like caricatures than anything else.<br /><br />Overall, this was super underwhelming and I'm pretty sure I gave myself an eye strain from rolling them so much. I might read the next book in the series to see if it improves, but I'm not getting my hopes up.</span>
  <a data-text-id="7929817682005585776" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_219445783" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/219445783" />
    <a title="Giselle" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4800103-giselle"><img alt="Giselle" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1310159877p2/4800103.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/219445783?book_show_action=true">Oct 05, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Giselle" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Giselle" href="/user/show/4800103-giselle">Giselle</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4800103-giselle?shelf=arc">arc</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4800103-giselle?shelf=ebook">ebook</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer219445783" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4646291842059503848">Ok, I have to gather my thoughts now, because this book has blown my mind! I absolutely loved it! This is my first book by Jennifer, but it definitely won't be my last. I will now stalk all of her work - beware! There is no wonder she has been getting rave reviews so far.<br/><br/>Obsidian gets us acquainted with Katy, who has just moved to a boring small town in West Virginia, and with not-so-boring Daemon who is the most arrogant <s>human</s> being she has ever met. And, lucky her (seriously! lucky her!), he l</span>
  <span id="freeText4646291842059503848" style="display:none">Ok, I have to gather my thoughts now, because this book has blown my mind! I absolutely loved it! This is my first book by Jennifer, but it definitely won't be my last. I will now stalk all of her work - beware! There is no wonder she has been getting rave reviews so far.<br /><br />Obsidian gets us acquainted with Katy, who has just moved to a boring small town in West Virginia, and with not-so-boring Daemon who is the most arrogant <s>human</s> being she has ever met. And, lucky her (seriously! lucky her!), he lives right next door. But at least his sister is great. When Katy finds out they're all aliens, though, her life kind of gets weird... a little.<br /><br />I instantly clicked with Katy- and not just because she is a book blogger even though that was awesome -, I found her to be a lot like me. Her reactions, her emotions, her attitude were all very realistic and I could completely relate to her. I particularly appreciated her reaction to finding out Daemon was an alien. First of all she actually HAD a reaction! Secondly, she questioned it. Much better than the "Oh so you're a (insert paranormal being here)? That's neat! So…*awkward silence* wanna make out?" reactions I've too often encountered. I loved her friendship with Dee. I think Dee is a great person and she's absolutely a lot of fun. I was also very happy with Katy's mom. She was down to earth, funny and caring. <br /><br />Daemon, yes, you need your own paragraph. Daemon is very likely going to end up on the top of everyone's "most sexiest male character" list. He is definitely on mine! He is irritating, infuriating and downright bullheaded, but holy damn is he ever hot! Daemon is incredibly protective of his sister and others of his race, but even when he was being… difficult, it wasn't without reason. He did love to push Katy's buttons and I mostly found it hilarious (though if I was her I would have punched him in the face). What came out of his mouth actually made me gape with disbelief a few times. Despite his <i>loveable</i> personality, he is an incredible character who fit extremely well with the story, even more-so with Katy, and gave it a very attractive vibe.<br /><br />Together, Daemon and Katy were fantastic. There was enough chemistry between them to give Marie Curie a run for her money! Their relationship was very love/hate. You never knew what Daemon's intentions were from one page to the next and it drove me crazy as much as it did Katy. However, you still couldn't help but adore him to pieces.<br /><br />Now for the plot, I found it was very exciting and well thought out. I really enjoyed Jennifer's take on the aliens in Obsidian: how they got there, their powers, the villains. It reminded me a bit of Smallville but it was still original and incredibly exciting. The book definitely does not lack in action and the climactic ending was completely fulfilling. <br /><br />I really have no negative aspect to mention in regards to this book. It was everything I was hoping for and more than I was expecting. No doubt that Jennifer is the up and coming author to watch out for!</span>
  <a data-text-id="4646291842059503848" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/207909391?book_show_action=true">Sep 13, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Maida»-(¯`v´¯)-»" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Maida»-(¯`v´¯)-»" href="/user/show/3161105-maida---v--">Maida»-(¯`v´¯)-»</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3161105-maida---v--?shelf=favorite-series">favorite-series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3161105-maida---v--?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3161105-maida---v--?shelf=my-heart-and-soul">my-heart-and-soul</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3161105-maida---v--?shelf=paperback-or-hc-i-own">paperback-or-hc-i-own</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3161105-maida---v--?shelf=book-boyfriends">book-boyfriends</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3161105-maida---v--?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3161105-maida---v--?shelf=action-romance-hot-stuff">action-romance-hot-stuff</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3161105-maida---v--?shelf=fantasy-romance-mystery-the-whole">fantasy-romance-mystery-the-whole</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3161105-maida---v--?shelf=alien-romance-say-what">alien-romance-say-what</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer207909391" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4618240363420313278">Okay so I waited for this book forever! I finally got it and read it non stop! It was amazing. I loved everything about it. The story line, plot, the idea of aliens, the characters, the romance and all the hilarious conversations between Daemon and Katy! LOL ;)<br/><br/>It was kind of sad about the whole situation with Dawson (Daemon's brother). I can't wait to find out his story. I just wish he comes back with Bethany somehow. My fave part about the book was the first conversation Daemon and Katy have. I</span>
  <span id="freeText4618240363420313278" style="display:none">Okay so I waited for this book forever! I finally got it and read it non stop! It was amazing. I loved everything about it. The story line, plot, the idea of aliens, the characters, the romance and all the hilarious conversations between Daemon and Katy! LOL ;)<br /><br />It was kind of sad about the whole situation with Dawson (Daemon's brother). I can't wait to find out his story. I just wish he comes back with Bethany somehow. My fave part about the book was the first conversation Daemon and Katy have. It was soooooo funny, I had tears in my eyes cause I was laughing so hard! ;p<br /><br />Katy is your average teenage girl. I love the fact the she doesn't get intimidated and has a mind of her own. She believes in what is right and follows her instincts and her heart (Daemon...LOL)! She was incredible in this story, no matter how many times Daemon pushed her away, she only tries harder to be in his and his sister's life! It was inspiring.<br /><br />Then we have Daemon.mmmmmmm! Well, the first thing that comes to my mind is YUMMMM and then he is sooo funny! Although, he puts up a "douchebag" face he actually cares for Katy...even if it's in his own weird way. I love him. Really, that's all I can say. I think I am addicted to his funny comments. It was funny, cause when I was reading I always was anticipating when he would say something hilarious and I would laugh my ass off! LMAO;)<br /><br />It was a really great, amazing, fantastic book! I can't wait to read Onyx next and see where Katy and Daemon's relationship goes. I just wish the waiting time was much less. If I had it my way...I'd get that damn book in this second!!! LOL ;) I recommend this book to everybody! It was crazy but sweet. A great way to pass your time! ;)</span>
  <a data-text-id="4618240363420313278" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('Vfp9MbZwoL0CUOCMl7PStAeuRyhfpd4qNDmbHsLz9grw2ycDWIdSzce6Adu/xc7L2wby/m+veDhuYozkDLwffA==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('ww8xbPx24bJyQKK+ZGwLUzXrGh8laSoO29VZ1fRY39ZmLmteEoETwreqQ+lMGhcs6UOvyRVjjByBjk4vOhc2oA==')})
  }

I also do NOT check my Goodreads email.<br/><br/>To email me, please use the below addy. <br/>jenniferlarmentrout@live.com<br/><br/># 1 New York Times and # 1 International Bestselling author Jennifer lives in Charles Town, West Virginia. All the rumors yo</span>
  <span id="freeText5102554580936146404" style="display:none">Hey Guys! Please note: I don't send out ARCs for review. If you're interested in reviewing a book of mine before release date, please contact the appropriate publisher. I also do NOT check my Goodreads email.<br /><br />To email me, please use the below addy. <br />jenniferlarmentrout@live.com<br /><br /># 1 New York Times and # 1 International Bestselling author Jennifer lives in Charles Town, West Virginia. All the rumors you’ve heard about her state aren’t true. When she’s not hard at work writing. she spends her time reading, watching really bad zombie movies, pretending to write, hanging out with her husband and her Jack Russell Loki. In early 2015, Jennifer was diagnosed with retinitis pigmentosa, a group of rare genetic disorders that involve a breakdown and death of cells in the retina, eventually resulting in loss of vision, among other complications. Due to this diagnosis, educating people on the varying degrees of blindness has become of passion of hers, right alongside writing, which she plans to do as long as she can. <br /><br />Her dreams of becoming an author started in algebra class, where she spent most of her time writing short stories….which explains her dismal grades in math. Jennifer writes young adult paranormal, science fiction, fantasy, and contemporary romance. She is published with Tor, HarperCollins Avon and William Morrow, Entangled Teen and Brazen, Disney/Hyperion and Harlequin Teen. Her Wicked Series has been optioned by PassionFlix. Jennifer has won numerous awards, including the 2013 Reviewers Choice Award for Wait for You, the 2015 Editor’s Pick for Fall With Me, and the 2014/2015 Moerser-Jugendbuch- Jury award for Obsidian. Her young adult romantic suspense novel DON’T LOOK BACK was a 2014 nominated Best in Young Adult Fiction by YALSA. Her adult romantic suspense novel TILL DEATH was a Amazon Editor’s Pick and iBook Book of the Month. Her young adult contemporary THE PROBLEM WITH FOREVER is a 2017 RITA Award Winner in Young Adult Fiction. She also writes Adult and New Adult contemporary and paranormal romance under the name J. Lynn. She is published by Entangled Brazen and HarperCollins.<br /><br />She is the owner of ApollyCon and The Origin Event, the successful annual events that features over hundred bestselling authors in Young Adult, New Adult, and Adult Fiction, panels, parties, and more.</span>
